<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">On March 21, 2024, ParkerVision, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release which reported financial and operating results for the year ended December 31, 2023. A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">The information contained in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1 hereto, has been &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to liability under that section. The information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing or document.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits.</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">(d) Exhibits:</div>

<div style="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;">&#160;</div>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; width: 100%;">

<body style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; padding: 0in 0.1in; cursor: auto;">
<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: right; font-size: 11pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt;"><b>&nbsp;Exhibit 99.1</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: center; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>ParkerVision Reports <a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="4" id="led328299F2023271678205059185">2023</a> Results</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>JACKSONVILLE</b><b>, Fla.,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="21x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="4" id="led328299F2023271678205039778">March 21, 2024</a> </b>&#8211;<b> </b>ParkerVision, Inc. (OTCQB: PRKR) (&#8220;ParkerVision&#8221;), a developer and marketer of technologies and products for wireless applications, today announced results for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="4" id="led328299F2023271678205050890">December 31, 2023</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Year End&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="4" id="led328299F2023271678205077734">2023</a> Summary and Recent Developments</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Since 2021, the Company has resolved patent infringement actions filed in the Western District of Texas against four defendants through patent license and settlement agreements, including one agreement reached in 2023 for which the Company received $25 million in gross proceeds.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company currently has active patent infringement cases in the Western District of Texas against MediaTek, Realtek, Texas Instruments, and NXP Semiconductors, as well as additional cases in the Western District of Texas against TCL and LGE that are currently stayed pending the outcome of the active cases.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 81pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">o</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">A jury trial is scheduled to begin in December 2024 in one of three active MediaTek cases with a jury trial in the first of two active Realtek cases scheduled to follow in January 2025.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In November 2023, the U.S. Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit&nbsp; ("CAFC") heard oral arguments in the Company's appeal from certain March 2022 Florida district court rulings dismissing the Company's long standing patent infringement case against Qualcomm. The CAFC's ruling is currently pending.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Lewis H. Titterton joined the ParkerVision board of directors in June 2023.&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Jeffrey Parker, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, commented, &#8220;The patent licensing and settlement proceeds received in 2023 generated $9.5 million in net income with no tax impact due to our ability to use prior net operating loss carryforwards.&nbsp; These proceeds also enabled the repayment of a significant portion of the principal on our secured contingent debt, $5 million in new borrowings at a lower rate of return to continue to support our business, and a restructuring of the prior secured contingent debt agreements.&nbsp; We continue to pursue licensing arrangements with third parties, both with and without enforcement actions."&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Mr. Parker continued, &#8220;We are preparing for two scheduled patent enforcement jury trials, one in a little over eight months from now against MediaTek and a second one a month later against Realtek.&nbsp; We also expect a ruling from the CAFC in the near future regarding our appeal in one of our cases against Qualcomm where the district court dismissed the case without a jury trial.&nbsp; We remain confident in our ability to demonstrate to a jury of our peers that our patented wireless technologies are being used without our permission and look forward to having our day in court with each of the defendants."</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt;">&#65279;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><br>
&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Financial Results</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Net income for&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="4" id="led328299F2023271678206231607">2023</a> was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="328303" data-tblv="4" id="led328303F2023271678206310573">$9.5</a> million compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x2" data-tblname="328303" data-tblv="4" id="led328303F2023271678206360495">$9.8</a> million for <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="4" id="led328299F2023271678206410215">2022</a>.&nbsp; Basic and diluted earnings per common share were $0.11 and $0.08 respectively for 2023, compared to basic and diluted loss per common share of $(0.13) in 2022.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 81pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">o</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The $19.3 million increase in earnings from 2022 to 2023 is primarily the result of&nbsp; a $24.1 million increase in revenue resulting from our patent enforcement and licensing efforts, a $2.6 million decrease in the loss related to the change in fair value of our contingent payment obligations, offset by a $7.0 million increase in operating expenses.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 124pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9632;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The increase in operating expenses from 2022 to 2023 is the result of a $9.6 million increase in contingent legal fees, offset by a $2.6 million decrease in share-based compensation expense.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 36px; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 24px; font-size: 11pt;">&#9679;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt; width: 1693px;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Our long-term liabilities decreased by $8.9 million in 2023 as a result of a $13.9 million repayment on our secured contingent payment obligation, offset by $5.0 million in new borrowings under that secured obligation.&nbsp;&nbsp; We also successfully extended the maturity dates of&nbsp; $1.2 million in convertible debt by at least two years.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 35px; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 23px; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt; width: 1695px;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">At December 31, 2023, we had $2.6 million in cash and cash equivalents and were able to reduce our accounts payable by 36%.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About ParkerVision</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision, Inc. invents, develops and licenses cutting-edge, proprietary radio-frequency (RF) technologies that enable wireless solution providers to make and sell advanced wireless communication products. &nbsp;ParkerVision is engaged in a number of patent enforcement actions in the U.S. to protect patented rights that it believes are broadly infringed by others. For more information, please visit www.parkervision.com.<i> (PRKR-I)</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Safe Harbor Statement</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><i>This press release contains forward-looking information. Readers are cautioned not to place undue reliance on any such forward-looking statements, each of which speaks only as of the date made. Such statements are subject to certain risks and uncertainties that are disclosed in the Company</i>&#8217;<i>s SEC reports, including the Form 10-K for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="4" id="led328299F2023271678206602212">December 31, 2023</a></i><i>. These risks and uncertainties could cause actual results to differ materially from those currently anticipated or projected.</i></p>
